is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board Game.","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9MTW9LBXZ72S","TileLayout":"Poster","Title":"Puppet Soccer Football 17","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.53865.13804643704815727.e3c125ca-25e3-4c20-a16b-b933c0cb79b4.0f0e7e17-dfa5-411b-bb87-5c025b1bb958","Height":300,"Width":300,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.53874.13804643704815727.ec11b630-7cda-44e4-9409-461303b610ef.90c6858e-f151-4058-9dc4-970d9083352f","Height":300,"Width":620,"BackgroundColor":"#FFFFFF","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Tasuta","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":2.0,"RatingsCount":"2","PackageFamilyNames":["21824TapFunGames.SoccerFootballLeague17_2cqc67e0wqwzw"],"ContentIds":["63fa5e9c-aad7-81a7-7b03-ccbc531ad63e","66d0621b-6bdb-34d0-e68e-8bfd5750fceb","9a26c7a2-3c90-5623-7290-1f57879bfc79"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC-arvuti","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Playing football has never been more exciting than in the new Soccer Football League! Arvuti rakendusi näitab tihti seda ettepanekut, kuid mängijad kasutavad füüsilist tekid tavaliselt liiguvad kuvaelma korraga.\r\n\r\nVõit\r\nMängu võitis pärast kõik kaardid on kolinud oma pakkidesse.\r\nErinevad arvuti versiooni Freecelli ajalt tegelema lahendamatu mängud.\r\n\r\n\r\nAjalugu\r\nÜks vanimaid esivanemad Freecelli Kaheksa Off. In juuni 1968 väljaanne Scientific American, Martin Gardner kirjeldatud tema \"Matemaatiline Games\" veerus mängu CL Baker, mis on sarnane FreeCell, välja arvatud see, kaardid lõpp on ehitatud ülikond mitte asendusliikme värve. Gardner kirjutas: \"Mäng oli õpetatud Baker isa, kes omakorda õppinud seda inglane 1920\". See variant on nüüdsest Baker mäng. FreeCell päritolu kohta võib ulatuvad veelgi 1945 ja Skandinaavia mäng nimega Napoleon St. Helena (mitte mängu Napoleon St. Helena, tuntud ka Forty Thieves).\r\n\r\nPaul Alfille muutunud Baker mängu, tehes kaardid ehitada vastavalt vahelduvad värvid, luues FreeCell. Ta rakendas esimest arvutipõhist versioon see Tugiisik programmeerimiskeele PLATO haridus arvutisüsteemi 1978. Alfille suutis näidata kergesti äratuntav pildikesed mängukaartide on 512 * 512 mustvalge ekraan on PLATO süsteemid.\r\n\r\nSee originaal FreeCell keskkond lubatud mängude 4C10 sambad ja 1C10 rakkude lisaks standard 8 * 4 mängu. Iga variant, programmi salvestatud pingerea mängijad pikima võitnud triibud. Seal oli ka turniiri süsteem, mis võimaldas inimestel konkureerida võita raske käsitsi korjatud tehingutest. Paul Alfille kirjeldab seda alguses FreeCell keskkonnas täpsemalt intervjuu 2000. aastast.\r\n\r\n\r\nLahendamine keerukus\r\nFreeCell mäng on pidev kaartide arv. See tähendab, et konstantse ajaga, inimene või arvuti võiks loetleda kõik võimalikud käigud on andnud start konfiguratsioon ja avastada võitnud komplekti liigub või, eeldades mängu ei saa lahendada, selle puudumisest. Teha huvitav keerukus analüüsides tuleb ehitada üldistatud versioon FreeCell mängu 4 * n kaardid. See üldistatud versioon mäng on NP-täielik; see on ebatõenäoline, et algoritm tõhusam kui brute-force otsing olemas, et saab leida lahendusi suvalise üldistatud FreeCell koosseisudes.\r\n\r\nSeal on 52! (St 52 faktoriaali), või umbes 8 * 1067 erinevat tehingutest. Kuid mõned mängud on tegelikult identsed teised, sest ülikonnad määratud kaardid on meelevaldsed ega veerge saab vahetada.
